Gardner je zapisal: »Igra je učil, da Baker ga je njegov oče, ki pa ga je naučil od Angleža v 1920.\" Ta varianta se zdaj imenuje Pekovski Game. Tam je bil tudi sistem, turnir, ki je omogočila ljudem, da tekmujejo za zmago težke ročno obirajo ukvarja. Paul Alfille opisuje ta zgodnje Kralj okolje, podrobneje v intervjuju iz leta 2000.\r\n\r\n\r\nReševalec kompleksnost\r\nKralj Igra ima konstantno število kartic. Če želite izvesti zanimivo analizo kompleksnosti moramo gradnjo vsesplošno različico Kralj igre s 4 * n kartic. Ta posplošena različica igre je NP-popolna; je malo verjetno, da obstaja kak algoritem učinkovitejše kot iskanje po Brutalni sile, ki lahko najdejo rešitev za samovoljne splošnih konfiguracije Kralj.\r\n\r\nObstaja 52! Easy on CPU and memory.\r\nIMPORTANT: uBlock Origin is completely unrelated to the site \"ublock.org\".\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nAn efficient blocker: easy on memory and CPU footprint, and yet can load and enforce thousands more filters than other popular blockers out there.\r\n\r\nUsage: The big power button in the popup is to permanently disable/enable uBlock Origin for the current web site. It applies to the current web site only, it is not a global power button.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nFlexible, it's more than an \"ad blocker\": it can also read and create filters from hosts files.\r\n\r\nOut of the box, these lists of filters are loaded and enforced:\r\n\r\n- EasyList\r\n- Peter Lowe’s Ad server list\r\n- EasyPrivacy\r\n- Malware domains\r\n\r\nMore lists are available for you to select if you wish:\r\n\r\n- Fanboy’s Enhanced Tracking List\r\n- Dan Pollock’s hosts file\r\n- hpHosts’s Ad and tracking servers\r\n- MVPS HOSTS\r\n- Spam404\r\n- And many others\r\n\r\nOf course, the more filters enabled, the higher the memory footprint. Yet, even after adding Fanboy's two extra lists, hpHosts’s Ad and tracking servers, uBlock Origin still has a lower memory footprint than other very popular blockers out there.\r\n\r\nAlso, be aware that selecting some of these extra lists may lead to higher likelihood of web site breakage -- especially those lists which are normally used as hosts file.\r\n\r\n***\r\n\r\nFree.\r\nOpen source with public license (GPLv3)\r\nFor users by users.\r\n\r\nIf ever you really do want to contribute something, think about the people working hard to maintain the filter lists you are using, which were made
